# Linear A Corpus, LLM-Oriented Reading Edition

This package reformats an open Linear A corpus into machine-friendly and retrieval-friendly forms. Linear A remains undeciphered; transliterations are conventional sign values and any glosses are limited source annotations, not a full translation.

## Apodoulou (3 inscriptions)

### APZa1
- Support: Stone vessel
- Context: Unknown
- Findspot: Unknown

```text
𐘱𐘳𐘚𐙕𐘉𐘱𐄁𐝫
```

Transliteration: JA-TA-I-*301-U-JA 𐄁

Gloss/notes: gives 𐄁

### APZa2
- Support: Stone vessel
- Context: Unknown
- Findspot: Unknown

```text
𐝫𐘅𐘤𐄁𐘚𐘢𐘅𐙁𐝫𐄁𐝫𐘚𐙂𐘰𐘅𐘹𐘅𐘃𐝫
𐝫𐘢𐘻𐘅𐘃𐄁𐘚𐘅𐘱𐘙𐘳𐝫𐄁𐝫𐘌𐄁
```

Transliteration: NA-SI 𐄁 I-PI-NA-MA 𐄁 I-KU-PA₃-NA-TU-NA-TE \n PI-MI-NA-TE 𐄁 I-NA-JA-RE-TA 𐄁 QA 𐄁

Gloss/notes: NA-SI 𐄁 a favour 𐄁 I-KU-PA₃-NA-TU-NA-TE \n PI-MI-NA-TE 𐄁 I-NA-JA-RE-TA 𐄁 QA 𐄁

### ARKH1a

- Findspot: Unknown

```text
𐘇𐘂𐝫

```

Transliteration: TA-PI 𐄁 \n QA \n KI \n 𐝫 𐄁 \n A-RA \n 𐝫 \n A-SU-MI-*118 \n NE 2 ¹⁄₂ \n A-PA \n MI-KI-SA-NE

Gloss/notes: TA-PI 𐄁 \n QA \n KI \n 𐝫 𐄁 \n A-RA \n 𐝫 \n A-SU-MI-*118 \n NE 2 ¹⁄₂ \n A-PA \n MI-KI-SA-NE
